+    (() => {
+      const palette = { dark: "#09090B", light: "#F5F5F4" };
+      const validThemes = new Set(["system", "dark", "light"]);
+      try {
+        const savedTheme = localStorage.getItem("mototrack-theme");
+        const mode = validThemes.has(savedTheme) ? savedTheme : "system";
+        const resolved =
+          mode === "system" && window.matchMedia && window.matchMedia("(prefers-color-scheme: dark)").matches

+        document.documentElement.dataset.resolvedTheme = resolved;
+        const meta = document.querySelector('meta[name="theme-color"]');

+        const manifest = document.querySelector('link[rel="manifest"]');

+            const manifestUrl = new URL(baseHref, window.location.origin);
+            manifestUrl.searchParams.set("mode", mode);
+            manifestUrl.searchParams.set("resolved", resolved);
+            manifest.setAttribute("href", manifestUrl.toString());

+      } catch (error) {
+        document.documentElement.dataset.theme = "system";
+        document.documentElement.dataset.resolvedTheme = "light";
+      }
+    })();

+                const field = container.querySelector('input, textarea, select');
